Role Summary

The Senior Backend Engineer is a crucial position within Vingcard | ASSA ABLOY, primarily responsible for designing, developing and maintaining robust backend solutions that power our innovative access control systems for hotels and adjacent markets. The role demands a deep understanding of backend technologies, including Spring Boot, Spring MVC, Java, and Kotlin. The candidate will work in a dynamic, cross-functional team to deliver high-quality software that enhances the functionality and performance of our products.

Job Location: Brasilia, Brazil

KEY Responsibilities

 Design, develop and maintain backend applications using Spring Boot, Spring MVC, Java, and Kotlin. 
 Collaborate with frontend developers to integrate user-facing elements using server-side logic. 
 Write clean, maintainable, and efficient code. 
 Contribute to all phases of the development lifecycle, from design to deployment. 
 Troubleshoot, debug, and optimize backend systems. 
 Ensure high performance and responsiveness of the application. 
 Maintain up-to-date knowledge of current backend technologies and best practices. 
 Participate in code reviews, providing feedback and suggestions for improvement. 
 Provide technical leadership and guidance to junior developers, helping them navigate technical challenges and grow in their careers. 
 Ensure adherence to best practices in software engineering, including code quality, testing, and documentation. 

Responsibilities And Authorities

 Authority to make technical decisions related to software architecture and design. 
 Access to all necessary information and tools to perform role effectively. 
 Responsibility for delivering high-quality software solutions on time and within budget. 
 Authority to mentor and provide career development support to junior developers. 
 Reporting to the R&D Manager for project assignments and career development. 

 Internal and External Contacts/Customers

Skills

 Experience with Git versioning systems.
